release making the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces Second Quarter 2022 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;August
9, 2022&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ --&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the six and three months ended&nbsp;June 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu, Chairman
and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented, &ldquo;Despite the negative impact associated with the resurgence of COVID-19 pandemic
to our business during the second quarter of 2022, we strived to provide high-quality products to our customers. As business activities
gradually return to normal, we expect to take the necessary steps to strengthen our business resilience and improve our competitive advantages
to prepare for growth opportunities ahead. With our dedicated team&rsquo;s effort and our long-term strategy of exploring growth opportunities
in the industry, we remain confident about our business fundamentals and potential to grow. Despite the challenging environment, we anticipate
to continue to execute our strategic initiatives, expand our business, and improve operating efficiency. In addition, we remain focused
on improving our products to meet the evolving demands of our customers and strengthen our relationship with customers. Looking ahead
to the remainder of 2022 and beyond, we believe we are well positioned to achieve our growth goals and create long-term values for shareholders.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Second Quarter 2022
Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: left; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Revenue</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the second quarter
of 2022, total revenue decreased by 31.7%, to&nbsp;approximately $31.79 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $46.53 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of CMP, offset printing paper and
tissue paper products.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 15.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $31.29 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.4% of total revenue for the second
quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $36.81million, or 79.1% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 65,585 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$477/tonne in the second quarter of 2022, compared to 73,998&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$497/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 14.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $25.85 million for the second quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $30.25
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 53,943 tonnes of regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$479/tonne during the second
quarter of 2022, compared to 60,507 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$500/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP
decreased by 17.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $5.44 million for the second quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $6.56
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 11,642 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$467/tonne for the second
quarter of 2022, compared to 13,491 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$486/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil&nbsp;for
the second quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$7.18 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 10,415 tonnes of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$690/tonne in the second quarter of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 83.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.41million for the second quarter of 2022, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$2.43 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 383 tonnes of tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,074/tonne for the second quarter
of 2022, compared to 2,196 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,106/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 19.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.09 million&nbsp;for the second quarter of 2022, from $0.11 million for the same period of
last year. The Company sold 3,014 thousand pieces of face masks for the second quarter of 2022, compared to 2,635 thousand pieces of face
masks for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross
Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 28.4%, to&nbsp;approximately
$31.15 million&nbsp;for the second quarter of 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $43.51 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The decrease
in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the decrease in sales quantity of regular CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products.&nbsp;
Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$459,&nbsp;$439,
$nil and&nbsp;$3,200, respectively, for the second quarter of 2022, compared to $475,&nbsp;$454,&nbsp;$567&nbsp;and&nbsp;$1,211, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $0.63
million&nbsp;for the second quarter of 2022, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $3.03 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 2.0% for the second quarter of 2022, compared to 6.5% for
the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products
and face mask products were 4.3%, 6.0%, nil%, -198.0% and 20.8%, respectively, for the second quarter of 2022, compared to 5.1%, 6.7%,
17.7%, -9.6% and 10.0%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) decreased by 28.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.87 million&nbsp;for the second quarter of
2022 from&nbsp;approximately $2.60 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $1.24 million&nbsp;for the second quarter of 2022, a decrease of 386.9%, from income from operations of&nbsp;approximately
$0.43 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 3.9% for the second quarter of 2022, compared to operating
income margin of 0.9% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$0.29 million, or loss per share of $0.003, for the second quarter of 2022, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $0.45 million,
or loss per share of $0.01, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$3.55 million&nbsp;for the second quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $9.03 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the first half of
2022, total revenue decreased by 33.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $47.27 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $70.74 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of CMP, offset printing paper and
tissue paper products.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">The following table summarizes
revenue, volume and ASP by product for the first half of 2022 and 2021, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 19.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $46.32 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.0% of total revenue for first half
of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $57.53million, or 81.3% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company sold 94,671
tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$489/tonne in first half of 2022, compared to 115,294&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$499/tonne in the
same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 17.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $38.95 million for first half of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $47.22 million
for the same period of last year. The Company sold 79,188 tonnes of regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$492/tonne during the first half of
2022, compared to 94,133 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$502/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased
by 28.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $7.36 million for the first half of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $10.31 million for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 15,483 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$476/tonne for the first half of 2022,
compared to 21,161tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$487/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil&nbsp;for
the first half of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$9.30 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 13,557 tonnes of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$686/tonne in the first half of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 78.0%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.81 million for the first half of 2022, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$3.68 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 780 tonnes of tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,038/tonne for the first half of
2022, compared to 3,317 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,109/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 5; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->5<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 39.8%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.14 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, from $0.24 million for the same period of last
year. The Company sold 12,664 thousand pieces of face masks for the first half of 2022, compared to 6,470 thousand pieces of face masks
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross
Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 29.7%, to&nbsp;approximately
$46.33 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $65.88 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The decrease
in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the decrease in sales quantity of CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products.&nbsp;
Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$469,&nbsp;$445,$nil
and&nbsp;$2,805, respectively, for the first half of 2022, compared to $470,&nbsp;$447,&nbsp;$562&nbsp;and&nbsp;$1,317, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $0.94
million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $4.86 million&nbsp;for the same period of last
year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 2.0% for the first half of 2022, compared to 6.9% for the same period
of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products and face mask
products were 4.6%, 6.5%, nil%, -170.2% and 24.2%, respectively, for the first half of 2022, compared to 6.3%, 8.3%, 18.1%, -18.7% and
14.8%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) increased by 0.3%, to&nbsp;approximately $5.17 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022
from&nbsp;approximately $5.15 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $4.19 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, an increase of 1331.9%, from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately
$0.29 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 8.9% for the first half of 2022, compared to operating
loss margin of 0.4% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$2.78 million, or loss per share of $0.03, for the first half of 2022, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $4.79 million, or loss
per share of $0.10, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$4.75 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $8.96 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and
Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of&nbsp;June 30, 2022, the Company had cash
and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party loans),
and long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $14.34million,&nbsp;$11.10million and&nbsp;$4.92million, respectively,
compared to approximately $11.20&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$13.52&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$2.98 million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December 31,
2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net accounts receivable
was&nbsp;approximately $3.82&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;June 30, 2022, compared to approximately&nbsp;$4.87&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December
31, 2021. Net inventory was approximately&nbsp;$6.63&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;June 30, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $5.84&nbsp;million
as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021. As of&nbsp;June 30, 2022, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately $48.45&nbsp;million and current
liabilities of&nbsp;approximately $17.33million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately $31.12&nbsp;million. This was compared
to current assets of approximately $55.52 million and current liabilities of approximately $20.43 million, resulting in a working capital
of approximately $35.09 million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately
$3.95million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, compared to net cash used in operating activities of approximately&nbsp;$15.57 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately $7.32 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022,
compared to approximately $0.17 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Net cash provided by financing activities was&nbsp;approximately
$6.67 million&nbsp;for the first half of 2022, compared to approximately $41.67 million for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging,
Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech
Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China.
Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three
categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding
and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
